pipeline in ArangoDB follows a multi-stage transformation and execution process:\\n\\n1. **PARSING STAGE**: The Parser class (arangod/Aql/Parser.h, Parser.cpp) is the entry point that parses the AQL query string into an Abstract Syntax Tree (AST). The Parser constructor takes a QueryContext, Ast, and QueryString, and generates the AST representation of the query.\\n\\n2. **OPTIMIZATION STAGE**: The Optimizer class (arangod/Aql/Optimizer.h, Optimizer.cpp) takes the AST and applies optimization rules to generate an optimized ExecutionPlan. The Optimizer constructor initializes with a ResourceMonitor and maxNumberOfPlans, and maintains a PlanList structure containing potential execution plans that are iteratively optimized.\\n\\n3. **EXECUTION PLAN INSTANTIATION**: The ExecutionEngine class (arangod/Aql/ExecutionEngine.h, ExecutionEngine.cpp) is responsible for instantiating the execution plan into actual execution blocks. The static method ExecutionEngine::instantiateFromPlan() creates ExecutionBlock instances from ExecutionNodes in the optimized plan. The ExecutionEngine manages the overall query execution lifecycle and coordinates data flow between blocks.\\n\\n4. **EXECUTION BLOCKS**: The ExecutionBlock class (arangod/Aql/ExecutionBlock.h, ExecutionBlock.cpp) represents the fundamental building blocks of query execution. Each ExecutionBlock corresponds to an operation in the execution plan (e.g., collection scan, filter, projection, join). ExecutionBlocks process data in batches (default batch size of 1000 rows) and communicate through AqlItemBlock structures. They follow a lifecycle of initialize() -> initializeCursor() -> execute() -> DESTRUCTOR.\\n\\n5. **STORAGE ENGINE INTERFACE**: The RocksDBCollection class (arangod/RocksDBEngine/RocksDBCollection.h, RocksDBCollection.cpp) implements the storage engine interface for data retrieval. It extends RocksDBMetaCollection and provides methods like getAllIterator() and getAnyIterator() to retrieve documents from RocksDB. RocksDBCollection manages document storage, indexes, and document-level operations through RocksDB transactions.\\n\\n6. **TRANSACTION MANAGEMENT**: The transaction::Methods class (arangod/Transaction/Methods.h, Methods.cpp) manages transaction contexts and isolation for queries. It maintains transaction state, handles lock management, and coordinates with the transaction::Manager (arangod/Transaction/Manager.h, Manager.cpp). The Manager tracks all active transactions and provides lifecycle management for both managed and standalone transactions.\\n\\nThe execution flow is:\\nAQL Query String → Parser → AST → Optimizer → ExecutionPlan → ExecutionEngine → ExecutionBlocks → RocksDBCollection (via transaction::Methods) → Data Retrieval from RocksDB\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4068,"cache_read_input_tokens":59939,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4068},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"1de35826-27f3-4197-a8d0-cec6a873486e","uuid":"8a5abd14-f835-4e11-8a22-010b9817d186"}
